## createReturnFulfillmentWorkflow

This workflow creates a fulfillment for a return.

## createShipmentWorkflow

This workflow creates shipments for a fulfillment.

### Steps

## createShippingOptionsWorkflow

This workflow creates one or more shipping options.

### Steps

___

## markFulfillmentAsDeliveredWorkflow

This workflow marks fulfillment as delivered.

### Steps

<WorkflowDiagram workflow={{"name":"markFulfillmentAsDeliveredWorkflow","steps":[{"type":"step","name":"useRemoteQueryStep","description":"This step fetches data across modules using the remote query.\n\nLearn more in the [Remote Query documentation](https://docs.medusajs.com/advanced-development/modules/remote-query).\n\n","link":"../../core_flows.Steps_Common/page.mdx#useremotequerystep","depth":1},{"type":"step","name":"validateFulfillmentDeliverabilityStep","description":"This step validates that if a fulfillment can be marked delivered","link":"../../core_flows.Workflows_Fulfillment/page.mdx#validatefulfillmentdeliverabilitystep","depth":2},{"type":"workflow","name":"updateFulfillmentWorkflow","description":"This workflow updates a fulfillment.","link":"../../core_flows.Workflows_Fulfillment/page.mdx#updatefulfillmentworkflow","depth":3}]}} />

This workflow updates one or more service zones.
